# CHANGELOG

## 2026-06-17

### Revision `working` - dev-erp кіөмҡ© л¶„лҘҳ нҒҗмҷҖ мһҘл¶Җ нҺҳмқҙм§Җ кі„м•Ҫ

- `status=unclassified` н• мқјмқ„ нҢҖ кіөмҡ© л¶„лҘҳ нҒҗлЎң лӘ…мӢңн•ҙ мқјл°ҳ нҢҖмӣҗлҸ„ лҜёл°°м • л©”мқј нҢҢмғқ н• мқјмқ„
  мЎ°нҡҢВ·нҷ•м •н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н•Ё. м •мӢқ н• мқј мЎ°нҡҢлҠ” кё°мЎҙмІҳлҹј ліёмқё лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ лІ”мң„лҘј мң м§Җ.
- лҜёл¶„лҘҳ н• мқј нҷ•м • мӢң лӢҙлӢ№мһҗлҘј н•Ёк»ҳ м ҖмһҘн•ҳкі , мһ…л Ҙмқҙ л№„м–ҙ мһҲмңјл©ҙ м¶”мІң лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ лҳҗлҠ” нҳ„мһ¬ лЎңк·ёмқё
  мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗлҘј кё°ліё лӢҙлӢ№мһҗлЎң кё°лЎқн•ҙ кіөмҡ© нҒҗм—җм„ң к°ңмқё мӢӨн–ү лӘ©лЎқмңјлЎң мһҗм—°мҠӨлҹҪкІҢ мқҙлҸҷн•ҳкІҢ н•Ё.
- `/api/items` мҷҖ `/api/mail` м—җ `page=1` нҺҳмқҙм§Җ мқ‘лӢө(`rows,total,limit,offset,has_more`)мқ„
  м¶”к°Җн•ҳкі , кё°мЎҙ л°°м—ҙ мқ‘лӢөмқҖ мң м§Җн•ҙ лӢӨлҘё нҷ”л©ҙ нҳёнҷҳм„ұмқ„ ліҙмЎҙ.
- н• мқј/л©”мқј нҷ”л©ҙм—җ мқҙм „В·лӢӨмқҢ нҺҳмқҙм§Җ м»ЁнҠёлЎӨкіј м •нҷ•н•ң мҙқлҹү н‘ңмӢңлҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ л©”мқјВ·н• мқјмқҙ кі„мҶҚ
  мҢ“м—¬лҸ„ кі м • 500кұҙ м ңн•ңм—җ к°Җл Өм§Җм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ н•Ё.
- лҜёл¶„лҘҳ м—°мІҙ м•ҢлҰј, м¶ңмІҳ л©”мқј/мҶҢмҠӨ/мҠӨл Ҳл“ң м¶”м Ғ н‘ңмӢң, м¶ңмІҳ ref кІҖмғүмқ„ ліҙк°•н•ҙ л©”мқјм—җм„ң нҢҢмғқлҗң
  мқјмқҙ м–ҙл””м„ң мӢңмһ‘лҗҗлҠ”м§Җ нҷ”л©ҙм—җм„ң м¶”м Ғн•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н•Ё.

### Revision `working` - dev-erp кё°мЎҙ л©”мқј мқҙл Ҙ 754кұҙ н• мқј мһҘл¶Җнҷ”

- кё°мЎҙ `_workmeta/*/reports/л©”мқј_мқҙл Ҙ/л©”мқј_мқҙл Ҙ.csv` 8к°ң мһҘл¶Җмқҳ 754к°ң л©”мқј мқҙл Ҙм—җм„ң
  `mailtask:<мқҙл ҘнӮӨ>` н• мқј мһҘл¶Җ н–үмқ„ мғқм„ұн•ҳкі  dev-ERP DBм—җ мҲҳмһ…н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н•Ё.
- л©”мқјм—җ лӘ…мӢң кё°н•ңмқҙ мһҲмңјл©ҙ н•ҙлӢ№ лӮ м§ңлҘј мҡ°м„  мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳкі , м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ мҲҳмӢ мқј+3мқј мІ« кІҖнҶ кё°н•ңкіј
  кё°н•ң+2мқј лҰ¬л§Ҳмқёл“ң/кёүн•ң мһ¬кІҖнҶ  л¬ёкө¬лҘј мһҘл¶Җм—җ лӮЁкё°лҸ„лЎқ `mail_to_task_ledger.mjs` лҘј ліҙк°•.
- `P00-000_INBOX` мҳҲм•Ҫ мҪ”л“ңлҘј dev-ERPмқҳ мқёл°•мҠӨ н”„лЎңм қнҠёлЎң мҲҳмһ…н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н•ҙ нҡҢмӮ¬ мқјл°ҳ/лҜён•ҙкІ°
  л©”мқјлҸ„ л©”мқј мӣҗмһҘкіј н• мқј мӣҗмһҘм—җм„ң лҲ„лқҪлҗҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ н•Ё.
- л©”мқј н–үмқҳ мҠӨл Ҳл“ң н—ӨлҚ” alias, мҶҢмҠӨ кі„ліҙ н•ҙмӢң, мғқм„ұлҹ°/к·ңм№ҷ, л©”мқјмҶҢмҠӨIDлҘј ліҙмЎҙн•ҙ
  л©”мқјвҶ’н• мқј м¶”м Ғм„ұмқ„ к°•нҷ”.

### Revision `working` - dev-erp кі„м •лі„ л©”мқјн•Ё л“ұлЎқ л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°

- `guild-hall:gateway:fetch:team` кіј `mail_fetch/team_cli.py` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ metadata-only
  `team_mailboxes.json` л“ұлЎқл¶Җмқҳ м—¬лҹ¬ л©”мқјн•Ёмқ„ мҲңнҡҢ мҲҳм§‘н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н•Ё. л©”мқјн•Ёлі„ cursor/dedupe/run
  лЎңк·ёлҘј л¶„лҰ¬н•ҳкі , нӣ„ліҙ IDмҷҖ л©”мқј нӣ„ліҙ л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°м—җлҸ„ mailbox scope лҘј л°ҳмҳҒ.
- `dev-erp:export-team-mailboxes` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ dev-ERP кі„м •мқҳ safe mailbox л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°м—җм„ң
  `team_mailboxes.json` л“ұлЎқл¶ҖлҘј мғқм„ұн•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н•Ё(л№„л°Җк°’ лҜёнҸ¬н•Ё).
- `core_account` м—җ л©”мқјн•Ё provider/env ref/enabled/status/last-fetch/error/summary л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°лҘј
  м¶”к°Җн•ҳкі , env ref лҠ” repo-relative нҸ¬мқён„°л§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ кІҖмҰқмқ„ м¶”к°Җ.
- кҙҖлҰ¬мһҗ кі„м • нҢЁл„җкіј `/api/accounts/mailbox` м—”л“ңнҸ¬мқёнҠём—җм„ң кі„м •лі„ л©”мқјн•Ё л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°лҘј
  м ҖмһҘн•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н•ҳлҗҳ password/token/secret к°’мқҖ л°ӣкұ°лӮҳ н‘ңмӢңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ.
- л©”мқј мһҘл¶Җ мҠӨмә”мқҙ `л©”мқјн•Ё` к°’мқ„ `core_mail.mailbox` лЎң ліҙмЎҙн•ҳкі , л©”мқјвҶ’н• мқј мһҘл¶Җ мғқм„ұмқҖ
  кё°ліём ҒмңјлЎң л©”мқјн•Ё мҲҳмӢ мһҗлҘј `м ңм•ҲлӢҙлӢ№мһҗ` лЎңл§Ң л„Јмңјл©° `--assign-mailbox-owner` мӮ¬мҡ© мӢңм—җл§Ң
  нҷ•м • `лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ` лЎң кё°лЎқ.
- нҢҖмӣҗ кі„м •мқҳ кё°ліё л©”мқј/кІҖмғү/н• мқј/лҢҖмӢңліҙл“ң мҡ”м•Ҫ/мөңк·ј мқҙлІӨнҠё мЎ°нҡҢлҠ” ліёмқё mailbox/лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ лІ”мң„лЎң
  мўҒнһҲкі , л©”мқј л°°м •В·лқјлІЁВ·мҠ№кІ© л°Ҹ н• мқј ліҖкІҪ мҡ”мІӯлҸ„ мһҗкё° лІ”мң„ л°–мқҙл©ҙ кұ°л¶Җн•ҳлҸ„лЎқ м„ңлІ„ мёЎ к°Җл“ңлҘј ліҙк°•.

### Revision `working` - dev-erp л©”мқј кё°л°ҳ н• мқј мһҗлҸҷнҷ” л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„° ліҙк°•

- л©”мқј нӣ„ліҙ вҶ’ н• мқј мһҘл¶Җ вҶ’ ERP мқёмһ… нқҗлҰ„м—җм„ң кІҖнҶ мғҒнғң, лқјмҡ°нҠё нӣ„ліҙ/мӢ лў°лҸ„, н•„мҡ” м—ӯн• В·м—ӯлҹү,
  м ңм•Ҳ лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ, мҶҢмҠӨ л©”мқј/нӣ„ліҙ/мҠӨл Ҳл“ң/к·ёлЈ№, мғқм„ұлҹ°/к·ңм№ҷ, лҸҷкё°нҷ” мғҒнғң/н•ҙмӢң/лҰ¬л№„м „мқ„
  ліҙмЎҙн•ҳлҸ„лЎқ н• мқј мһҘл¶ҖмҷҖ `core_item` л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°лҘј нҷ•мһҘ.
- н• мқј мһҘл¶Җ мқёмһ…мқҖ кё°мЎҙ н• мқјмқ„ мЎ°мҡ©нһҲ лҚ®м–ҙм“°м§Җ м•Ҡкі  н•ҙмӢң м°Ёмқҙк°Җ лӮҳл©ҙ
  `conflict` лЎң н‘ңмӢңн•ҙ мӮ¬лһҢ мҲҳм • мқҙл Ҙмқ„ ліҙнҳён•ҳлҸ„лЎқ м •лҰ¬.
- dev-erp нҷ”л©ҙмқҳ н• мқј лӘ©лЎқВ·н—ҲлёҢВ·лҜёл¶„лҘҳ м№ҙл“ңм—җ кІҖнҶ /лқјмҡ°нҠё/лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ/лҸҷкё°нҷ” нһҢнҠёлҘј н‘ңмӢңн•ҙ
  мһҗлҸҷ мғқм„ұлҗң н• мқјмқ„ мӮ¬лһҢмқҙ л°”лЎң кІҖнҶ н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н•Ё.
- gateway л©”мқј нӣ„ліҙ/мғҒнғң м§‘кі„к°Җ мӣҗл¬ёВ·мІЁл¶ҖлӘ… м—Ҷмқҙ кө¬мЎ°нҷ”лҗң нӣ„ліҙ л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°л§Ң м „лӢ¬н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ ліҙк°•.

### Revision `working` - dev-erp м§ҖмӢқ лҢҖл¶„лҘҳ л¶„лҰ¬ + л¶„м•ј 4к·ёлЈ№ + canon л·°м–ҙ

- `м§ҖмӢқВ·м§Җмӣҗ`(лҢҖлҸ„м„ңкҙҖ) лҢҖл¶„лҘҳлҘј **м§ҖмӢқ**(м „мҠ№ м„ңкі ) / **лҸ„кө¬В·м§Җмӣҗ**(м ңмһ‘ лҸ„кө¬) **л‘җ
  лҢҖл¶„лҘҳлЎң л¶„лҰ¬**.
- **м§ҖмӢқ**: л¶„м•ј 4к·ёлЈ№мқ„ к°ҖлЎң м„ңлёҢнғӯ(н‘ңмӨҖВ·к·ңкІ©м§‘ / л¶„м•ј кё°мҲ  / м§ҖмӢқВ·RAG л°©лІ• /
  мҡҙмҳҒ к·ңлІ”В·көҗлҰ¬) + кІҖмғүВ·м§Җм№Ё. к°Ғ к·ёлЈ№мқҳ canon н•ӯлӘ©мқ„ **мҷјмӘҪм—җ лҸҷм Ғ лӮҳм—ҙ**(`.registry/
  knowledge` лҰ¬лҚ” мҶҢл№„), нҒҙлҰӯн•ҳл©ҙ н•ӯлӘ© л·°м–ҙ(м ңлӘ©В·л¶„м•јВ·мҡ”м•ҪВ·кіөк°ң м¶ңмІҳВ·мҶҢмҠӨм№ҙл“ң нҸ¬мқён„°)
  лҳҗлҠ” к·ёлЈ№ м№ҙл“ң лӘ©лЎқ. мӣҗл¬ё лҜём ҖмһҘ.
- лқјлІЁ/м№ҙн…Ңкі лҰ¬лҠ” лӘЁл“ңлі„(business/fantasy). мһ”мЎҙ `kb` localStorage лҠ” м•Ҳм „н•ҳкІҢ лҰ¬м…Ӣ.

### Revision `working` - dev-erp л©”мқј мқҙл Ҙ н”„лЎңм қнҠёлі„ кө¬л¶„(кё°ліё)

- л©”мқј мқҙл Ҙмқҙ **кё°ліёмңјлЎң н”„лЎңм қнҠёлі„ к·ёлЈ№**(н—ӨлҚ”=н”„лЎңм қнҠё м№©+м ңлӘ©+кұҙмҲҳ)мңјлЎң кө¬л¶„лҗЁ.
  нҲҙл°” нҶ кёҖлЎң н”„лЎңм қнҠёлі„ вҮ„ лӮ м§ңлі„ м „нҷҳ. лҜёл¶„лҘҳ/INBOX к·ёлЈ№мқҖ л§Ё м•„лһҳ, к·ёлЈ№мқҖ мөңмӢ  л©”мқј мҲң.
- мӢӨм ң л¶ҷмқҖ лқјлІЁ(мҲҳлҸҷ мғү лқјлІЁ)мқҖ н–үм—җ м№©мңјлЎң н‘ңмӢң вҖ” н”„лЎңм қнҠёлі„ к·ёлЈ№м—җм„  н”„лЎңм қнҠё м№©мқҙ
  н—ӨлҚ”лЎң мҳ¬лқјк°Җ н–үмқҖ л¶Җк°Җ лқјлІЁл§Ң н‘ңмӢң.
- л©”мқј л¶„лҘҳ м°Ёмӣҗ(мҠӨнӮӨл§Ҳ кё°мӨҖ): н”„лЎңм қнҠё(мЈјл Ҙ)В·л°©н–Ҙ(л°ӣмқҖ/ліҙлӮё)В·мғҒлҢҖ(counterpart)В·мҲҳлҸҷ лқјлІЁВ·
  SE лӢЁкі„(stage_code)В·л©”мқјн•Ё(mailbox, лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ н”„лЎқмӢң). лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ(лӮҙл¶Җ)лҠ” л©”мқј м§Ғм ‘ н•„л“ңк°Җ м•„лӢҲлқј
  н•  мқј мҠ№кІ© нӣ„ л¶Җм—¬.

### Revision `working` - dev-erp мқёмҰқ лІҪ + мІ« нҺҳмқҙм§Җ(лӢ¬л№ӣ кёёл“ң мһ…м„ұ)

- dev-erp к°Җ нҢҖ лӘЁл“ң(кі„м • 1к°ң мқҙмғҒ)м—җм„ң **лЎңк·ёмқё м—ҶмқҙлҠ” м•ұВ·лҚ°мқҙн„°лҘј ліј мҲҳ м—ҶкІҢ** лҗЁ.
  лҜёмқёмҰқмқҙл©ҙ н’ҖмҠӨнҒ¬лҰ° мІ« нҺҳмқҙм§Җ(кІҢмқҙнҠё)л§Ң н‘ңмӢң: мІ« мӢӨн–ү=кёёл“ңл§ҲмҠӨн„° м°Ҫм„Ө(bootstrap),
  мқҙнӣ„=мһ…м„ұ(лЎңк·ёмқё)В·кёёл“ң к°Җмһ…(нҡҢмӣҗк°Җмһ…) нғӯ. **лӘЁл“ңлі„ мІ« нҷ”л©ҙ мҠӨнӮЁ** вҖ” нҢҗнғҖм§Җ=лӢ¬л№ӣ
  м•јк°„(лӢ¬В·лі„В·м•Ҳк°ңВ·лҠҘм„ ), мӢӨл¬ҙ=м „л¬ёк°Җмҡ© нқ° м№ҙл“ң(л„Өмқҙл№„). кІҢмқҙнҠё мҡ°мғҒлӢЁ нҶ кёҖлЎң м „нҷҳ.
- м„ңлІ„: GET мқҪкё°лҸ„ лҜёмқёмҰқ м°ЁлӢЁ(мў…м „м—” м“°кё°л§Ң м°ЁлӢЁ). лһңл”©м—җ н•„мҡ”н•ң л№„лҜјк°җ л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°
  (`/api/me`В·`/api/auth/*`В·`/api/health`В·`/api/lexicon`В·`/api/modules`)л§Ң мҳҲмҷё. `/api/health`
  мқҳ counts(лҚ°мқҙн„° к·ңлӘЁ)лҠ” лҜёмқёмҰқм—” мҲЁк№Җ.
- кёёл“ңмӣҗ мһҗк°Җ к°Җмһ… м—”л“ңнҸ¬мқёнҠё `/api/auth/register` м¶”к°Җ(member м—ӯн• , localhost л°”мқёл”©
  м „мҡ©мңјлЎң м•Ҳм „ вҖ” мҷёл¶Җ л…ём¶ң мӢң мҙҲлҢҖмҪ”л“ң/кҙҖлҰ¬мһҗ мҠ№мқёмңјлЎң м ңн•ң к¶ҢмһҘ). к°Җмһ…мқҖ
  `account_register` мқҙлІӨнҠёлЎң кё°лЎқ(к°җмӮ¬лЎңк·ё "нҡҢмӣҗк°Җмһ…").

## 2026-06-16

### Revision `working` - gateway mail history Python 3.9 compatibility

- Changed the project mail history ICS writer to use `Path.open(...,
  newline="")` instead of `Path.write_text(..., newline="")`, preserving
  explicit ICS line endings on Python 3.9 runtimes used by the mail-fetch test
  harness.

### Revision `working` - workspace-system report command added

- Added `guild-hall:workspace-system:report` so another PC can create a
  metadata-only `_workspaces/system` inventory report without pasting a long
  prompt.
- The report command writes JSON, Markdown, and CSV under
  `_workmeta/system/reports/workspace_system_inventory/<timestamp>_<node_id>/`
  and keeps payload bodies, local absolute paths, secrets, and workspace
  mutations out of the capture.
- Updated the workspace path identity and system migration runbooks to make the
  report folder the normal private evidence packet for cross-PC comparison.

### Revision `working` - workspace-system full scan inventory hardened

- Changed `guild-hall:workspace-system:inventory` so the default metadata
  inventory is an unrestricted recursive scan instead of a bounded sample.
- Added `scan_policy`, row-level `scan_complete`/`scan_limited` fields, and
  activation blockers for any bounded inventory result.
- Split project-coded reference payload folders such as
  `p25_054_reference_payloads` into `project_reference_payload_review` so they
  require owner mapping to a project payload relocation/reference surface rather
  than direct project-root movement.
- Updated workspace migration docs and tests so full-scan evidence is required
  before `_workspaces/system` migration or junction activation decisions.

### Revision `working` - system workspace tool-worker procedure saved

  `_workspaces/system` junction preflight checks.

  Allegro, Cadence, and OrCAD stay PC-local under `_workspaces/_local/<node_id>/...`
  or an owner-approved OS/tool location.
- Documented that only owner-classified outputs move to shared

  execution evidence stays in `_workmeta` as metadata only.

  shared-tree build, upload, delete, or permission changes.

  point to `_workspaces/_local/<node_id>/...` or owner-approved OS/tool
  locations, while reinstallable repo tools remain a separate bootstrap flow.

### Revision `working` - ERP/BOM кі„мёө кө¬мЎ° м§ҖлҸ„ м¶”к°Җ

  as a public-safe hierarchy map that reads Soulforge like an ERP/BOM:
  canon roots, registry entries, workflow/party catalogs, dev-erp runtime
  modules, widget/API/table layers, knowledge/RAG layers, and private/worksite
  boundaries.

  review starts from the foundation document index.
- Kept private payloads, mail bodies, attachments, local database contents,
  and secret values out of the public document; protected surfaces are described
  by role and repo-relative path only.

### Revision `working` - workspace system inventory gate added

- Added a read-only `_workspaces/system` inventory/classification gate through
  `guild-hall:workspace-system:inventory` and `validate:workspace-system`.
- Added deterministic classes for shared generated views, fixture candidates,
  project moves, knowledge moves, PC-local runtime/tools, cache/temp files,
  repo promotion review, conflicts, and unknown review rows.
- Blocked default RAG and knowledge graph writes to `_workspaces/system/**`
  while the `system` binding is still planned or the local path is not a link;
  PC-local temporary outputs must use `_workspaces/_local/<node_id>/system/**`.
- Updated `docs/ws.md` so other PCs start from the inventory gate and produce a
  dry-run cleanup plan without file mutation or host-local path leakage.

### Revision `working` - workspace path identity policy fixed

- Added a public workspace path identity policy so the same `_workspaces/<name>`
  path cannot mean different physical folders on different PCs unless it is
  explicitly under `_workspaces/_local/<node_id>/`.
- Reclassified `_workspaces/system` as a path-identity controlled shared system
  view, with pre-migration local copies preserved under
  `_workspaces/_local_hold/system/<timestamp>_<node_id>/`.
- Updated workspace, installation, knowledge graph, RAG, Obsidian export, and
  short PC handoff docs so default system outputs use the shared view and
  PC-local experiments use `_workspaces/_local/<node_id>/system/...`.
- Updated workspace junction audit and RAG/knowledge graph path guards to
  recognize `SE_TEMPLATE_LIBRARY`, `_local`, and `_local_hold` boundaries
  without allowing arbitrary `_workspaces` aliases.

### Revision `working` - workspace system check prompt shortcut

- Added `docs/ws.md` as a short hand-typed prompt entry for checking
  `_workspaces/system` or `Systems` sharing/junction drift on another PC.
- The prompt requires repo-relative reporting only, forbids local absolute path
  recording and secret/raw payload inspection, and limits the run to diagnosis
  plus dry-run repair planning unless the owner separately approves mutation.
- Expanded the prompt from diagnosis-only to a per-PC cleanup planning flow:
  classify local workspace-system entries, produce a dry-run cleanup plan, and
  keep all mutation behind explicit owner approval.
- Reframed the prompt goal so each PC drives toward `_workspaces/system` as the
  final junction path: preserve any existing local folder under a repo-relative
  hold location, create the junction only after explicit owner approval, and
  keep shared target paths out of reports.

  лЎңм§ҒмқҖ н•ҳмң„ л””л үнҶ лҰ¬ л¬ҙмӢңлқј мһҗм—° м°ЁнҸҗ. лЎңл“ңл§ө м ҖмһҘ к·ңм№ҷм—җ 1мӨ„ л“ұмһ¬.

  (used_refs/data_label/project_ref/actor) м»ӨлІ„лҰ¬м§Җ к°җмӮ¬, мқҪкё° м „мҡ©,
  --min кІҢмқҙнҠё мҳөм…ҳ. мІ« к°җмӮ¬лЎң view мқҙлІӨнҠёмқҳ project_ref кІ°мҶҗмқ„ л°ңкІ¬н•ҙ
  logView м—җ м°Ёмӣҗ м¶”к°Җ.

## 2026-06-13

### Revision `working` - system workspace drift migration runbook added

- Added `docs/architecture/workspace/SYSTEM_WORKSPACE_SYNC_MIGRATION_V0.md`
  as a public-safe coordination runbook for resolving drift in
  `_workspaces/system/` across multiple PCs before deciding whether the
  folder should remain local-only or become an owner-approved shared junction.
- The runbook defines a freeze, metadata-only manifest inventory, hash-based
  comparison classes, conflict handling, shared-root decision points, and
  public/private boundaries without exposing actual workspace files, PC names,
  local absolute paths, cloud account details, raw payloads, or secrets.
- Linked the runbook from `docs/architecture/workspace/README.md` so the team
  can find the migration status and procedure from GitHub.

  scope-driven unless the manager packet sets a specific limit.

  can write metadata-only usage records only when `--record-usage` and a safe

- Added `.registry/skills/post_development_review_gate` plus the installed Codex bridge `soulforge-post-development-review-gate` for consistent task-closing invocation.
- Locked the review gate workflow profile policy to conservative `gpt-5.5 / xhigh / auditor` final acceptance review instead of cost optimization.
- Made root UI lint/done-check scripts set the canonical root through a Node wrapper instead of Unix-only environment assignment.
- Updated the UI theme package smoke test and UI workspace wrapper so `npm pack` / UI scripts run through direct `npm.cmd` on Windows and direct `npm` elsewhere, avoiding shell quoting drift.

### Revision `working` - PCB layout guide extraction workflow added

- Registered the workflow in `.workflow/index.yaml` while keeping runtime part folders, extracted vendor text, figures, tables, and supplemental downloads outside public canon.
- Added token-control gates so PDF files are indexed and filtered into layout candidate spans before AI synthesis reads them.
- Added official supplemental-source download gates for missing layout guidance, with PDF/ZIP magic validation, source URL, byte size, and SHA256 requirements.
- Evolved the figure/table stage to use separate extraction tools by signal type: PyMuPDF for layout-candidate page/context PNG renders, Camelot strict quality-filtered Markdown tables, and pdfplumber only as a raw fallback candidate extractor.
- Clarified figure/table source-map and manifest records, including strict-vs-raw table counts, tool versions, output checksums, extraction warnings, and separate raw candidate folders.
- Added a layout-only promotion stage so PCB-layout-relevant visuals and tables are copied into dedicated `layout_only/` folders while software/setup/noisy candidates remain as context evidence with rejection reasons.
- Reworked figure capture policy so layout-only images must come from `layout_guide.md` cited evidence rather than earlier keyword-only candidate pages.
- Updated cited figure capture so `layout_only/` stores one full-page PNG per unique `layout_guide.md` cited source page, with repeated citations deduplicated and older cited-region crops retained only as runtime context evidence.
- Corrected cited figure output placement so current full-page PNGs live directly under `Layout Guide/figures/`; `figures/layout_only/` is no longer the figure output folder.
- Registered `component_pcb_layout_guide_extraction` as an owner-accepted usable workflow canon entry, with runtime vendor content and generated figures remaining project-local.

### Revision `working` - EXP XML component materials workflow added

- Added `.workflow/exp_xml_component_materials/` as a pilot-ready workflow for parsing a project-provided `EXP.xml` and collecting official datasheets plus EVAL/reference-design files into per-component `DATA Sheet` and `EVAL` folders.
- Registered the workflow in `.workflow/index.yaml` while keeping real EXP.xml contents, downloaded PDFs, PCB archives, credentials, and project-local run truth outside public canon.
- Added a project binding template for output folder shape, official-source download policy, checksum/source manifests, and review queues for ambiguous part identities or gated vendor material.
- Piloted the workflow against a concrete Cadence Capture EXP.xml, confirmed `PartInst` as the placed-component extraction node, and saved official Analog Devices PDF/ZIP materials into the project-local material tree.
- Tightened the workflow completion gate so source links and `.url` shortcuts are not accepted as downloads; actual files with byte size, content type or magic check, and SHA256 are required.
- Evolved the workflow with a larger Cadence Capture fixture, adding DOM-failure parser fallback, Package/SymbolUserProp identity recovery for placeholder part values, generic-passive review queue handling, and strict PDF/ZIP payload validation.

## 2026-05-11

### Revision `working` - device system diagram workflow canon entry added

- Added `.workflow/device_system_diagram_generation/` as an owner-accepted usable workflow for generating editable draw.io device system diagrams from one Markdown input and deriving SVG, PPTX, and PNG outputs.
- Registered the workflow in `.workflow/index.yaml` while keeping project-local paths, REF packets, raw candidates, and run evidence outside the public workflow canon.
- Marked the workflow as usable for project execution and timing checks, not strict REF canon-ready; future REF matching requires a non-oracle schema/source packet or owner-approved acceptance contract update.

- pending monster display sample cap мқ„ 24кұҙмңјлЎң мҳ¬л Ө нҳ„мһ¬ 18кұҙ к·ңлӘЁмқҳ мһ‘м „нҢҗ н‘ңмӢңк°Җ truncation м—Ҷмқҙ к°ҖлҠҘн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- UI Dungeon Map мқҖ snapshot мқҳ sanitized pending monster item л§Ң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҙ groupлі„ м„№м…ҳмңјлЎң н‘ңмӢңн•ҳл©° raw mail body/html/source quote/raw ref/attachment к°’мқҖ кі„мҶҚ м ңмҷён•ңлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - мһ‘м „нҢҗ pending monster snapshot мҡ”м•Ҫ м¶”к°Җ

- snapshot gateway projection мқҙ `intake_inbox/*/monsters.json` мқҳ pending/blocked monster лҘј м ңн•ңлҗң summary лЎң м§‘кі„н•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- UI Dungeon Map мқҳ Monster Gate м—җ pending monster count мҷҖ sample card лҘј н‘ңмӢңн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- snapshot кіј UI мқ‘лӢөмқҖ body/html/source quote/raw ref/attachment ref/provider id мӣҗл¬ёмқ„ ліөм ңн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  fixture кё°л°ҳ test лЎң л№„л…ём¶ңмқ„ кі м •н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - mail_candidate мҠ№кІ© лӘ…л № м¶”к°Җ

- `guild-hall:gateway:mail-candidate:list` мҷҖ `guild-hall:gateway:mail-candidate:promote` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ local-only mail candidate лҘј `mail_intake_request` payload лЎң мҠ№кІ©н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- promotion output мқҖ mailbox event/raw pointer мҷҖ кё°ліё `unknown_monster` 1кұҙмқ„ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳлҗҳ body/html/raw provider payload/мІЁл¶ҖлӘ…/мІЁл¶Җ URL/secret мқҖ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- mail candidate promotion кі„м•Ҫкіј public-safe request sample мқ„ л¬ём„ңнҷ”н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - mail_candidate нӣ„ліҙ нҒҗ м¶”к°Җ

- gateway mail fetch к°Җ fresh mail event лҘј mailbox event JSONL м—җ м ҖмһҘн•ң л’Ө, `mail` bucket event лҘј local-only `mail_candidate` queue м—җ м Ғмһ¬н•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- нӣ„ліҙ queue item мқҖ source event pointer, subject, sender, мҲҳмӢ мһҗ/мІЁл¶Җ count, classification summary л§Ң лӢҙкі  body/html/raw/мІЁл¶ҖлӘ…/мІЁл¶Җ URL/secret мқҖ м ңмҷён•ңлӢӨ.
- `MAIL_CANDIDATE_QUEUE_V0.md` мҷҖ public-safe sample мқ„ м¶”к°Җн•ҙ лӢӨлҘё PC к°Җ мӢӨм ң `guild_hall/state/**` мҡҙмҳҒ лҚ°мқҙн„° м—Ҷмқҙ queue shape лҘј мһ¬нҳ„н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - gateway index stale нҢҗм • ліҙк°•

- `intake_inbox` monster index manifest к°Җ `monsters.json` мқҳ mtime millisecond л§Ң ліҙм§Җ м•Ҡкі  size/sha256 fingerprint лҸ„ нҷ•мқён•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- к°ҷмқҖ tick м•Ҳм—җм„ң monster нҢҢмқјмқҙ к°ұмӢ лҸјлҸ„ stale manifest лҘј мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ gateway validation flake лҘј мӨ„мҳҖлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - node role public contract guard м¶”к°Җ

- лӘЁл“  PC clone м—җм„ң local `node_identity.yaml` мқҳ `primary_writer.public_repo` лҘј кё°мӨҖмңјлЎң protected public contract л¬ём„ң ліҖкІҪмқ„ кІҖмӮ¬н•ҳлҠ” `validate:role-boundary` лҘј м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- root `validate` / `done:check` к°Җ role-boundary guard лҘј лЁјм Җ мӢӨн–үн•ҙ, public repo primary к°Җ м•„лӢҢ node мқҳ м „м—ӯ кі„м•Ҫ л¬ём„ң мҠ№кІ© ліҖкІҪмқ„ кё°ліё м°ЁлӢЁн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- `MULTI_PC_DEVELOPMENT_V0.md` м—җ protected public contract кІҪлЎңмҷҖ owner мҠ№мқё override к·ңм№ҷмқ„ лӘ…мӢңн–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - skill first-build кІҖмҰқ кІҢмқҙнҠё лӘ…мӢң

- Soulforge м—җм„ң skill мқ„ мғҲлЎң л§Ңл“Өкұ°лӮҳ мҲҳм •н•  л•Ң нҢҢмқј мғқм„ұл§ҢмңјлЎң мҷ„лЈҢ ліҙкі н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі , validator мҷҖ fresh-context evaluator review лҘј кұ°м№ң л’Ө ліҙкі н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ project-level мӢӨн–ү кі„м•Ҫм—җ лӘ…мӢңн–ҲлӢӨ.
- subagent лҠ” нҳ„мһ¬ мӢӨн–ү нҷҳкІҪм—җм„ң н—Ҳмҡ©лҗҳкі  мӮ¬мҡ© к°ҖлҠҘн•ң кІҪмҡ°м—җл§Ң м“°л©°, л¶Ҳк°ҖлҠҘн•ң кІҪмҡ°м—җлҠ” лі„лҸ„ мғҲ м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё evaluator session лҳҗлҠ” мҲҳлҸҷ evaluator checklist лЎң лҢҖмІҙн•ҳкі  н•ңкі„лҘј ліҙкі н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - private-state changelog л§ҒнҒ¬ кІҖмӮ¬ ліҙм •

- `CHANGELOG_POLICY_V0.md` мқҳ private repo changelog м°ёмЎ°лҘј public CI к°Җ л”°лқјк°Җм•ј н•ҳлҠ” мғҒлҢҖ л§ҒнҒ¬к°Җ м•„лӢҲлқј local path лҰ¬н„°лҹҙлЎң н‘ңмӢңн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- `private-state/CHANGELOG.md` лҠ” owner-only nested private repo н‘ңл©ҙмқҙлҜҖлЎң public docs link check лҢҖмғҒм—җ л„Јм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” кІҪкі„лҘј лӘ…нҷ•нһҲ н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - mail_received Telegram brief v0 м¶”к°Җ

- gateway notify event set м—җ `mail_received` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҳкі , mail fetch к°Җ fresh event лҘј materialize н•ң л’Ө `town_crier` queue м—җ н•ңкөӯм–ҙ Telegram brief request лҘј м Ғмһ¬н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- `mail_received` brief лҠ” source, subject, мІ« л°ңмӢ мһҗ, мІЁл¶Җ к°ңмҲҳ, мҲҳмӢ  мӢңк°Ғ, лӢӨмқҢ н–үлҸҷл§Ң лӢҙкі  body/html/мІЁл¶Җ мӣҗл¬ё/URL/secret мқҖ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ formatter мҷҖ н…ҢмҠӨнҠёлҘј м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- Telegram brief format л¬ём„ңм—җ н•ңкөӯм–ҙ/Siri м№ңнҷ” кіөнҶө мӣҗм№ҷкіј `mail_received` н‘ңмӢң к·ңм№ҷмқ„ м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - workmeta system surface м ңмҷё

- snapshot project scan мқҙ `_workmeta/system/**` к°ҷмқҖ private metadata repo лӮҙл¶Җ мҡҙмҳҒ кё°лЎқмқ„ project нӣ„ліҙлЎң мҳӨмқён•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ м ңмҷён–ҲлӢӨ.
- `WORKMETA_RESOLVE_CONTRACT_V0.md` м—җ `_workmeta/system/` мқҖ node/system smoke кё°лЎқмҡ© non-project support surface лқјкі  лӘ…мӢңн–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - tool PC owner-with-state м—ӯн•  ліҙк°•

- кі м„ұлҠҘ `tool_pc` лҘј skill м ңмһ‘ м „мҡ©мқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј project metadata лҘј мқҪкі  м“°лҠ” tool-bound м„Өкі„ мһ‘м—… node лЎң лӘ…мӢңн–ҲлӢӨ.
- `MULTI_PC_DEVELOPMENT_V0.md` м—җ `tool_pc` мқҳ `_workspaces` / `_workmeta` writer кІҪкі„мҷҖ мӨ‘ліө л°©м§Җ к·ңм№ҷмқ„ м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- `TOOL_PC_BOOTSTRAP_PROMPT_V0.md` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ кі м„ұлҠҘ PC лҘј `owner-with-state` лЎң мһ¬м„Өм •н•ҳкі  нҡҢлЎңм„Өкі„/PCBArtwork/tool run evidence лҘј кё°лЎқн•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - gateway env мғҒлҢҖ кІҪлЎң н•ҙм„қ ліҙк°•

- `gateway:fetch:healthcheck`, state backup/restore, retention cleanup мқҙ `EMAIL_FETCH_RUNTIME_DIR` мҷҖ `EMAIL_FETCH_INBOX_ROOT` мқҳ мғҒлҢҖ кІҪлЎңлҘј env нҢҢмқј мң„м№ҳ кё°мӨҖмңјлЎң н•ҙм„қн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- always-on node мқҳ post-review smoke м—җм„ң мғҒлҢҖ runtime кІҪлЎңк°Җ repo л°–мңјлЎң н•ҙм„қлҗҳм–ҙ healthcheck/healer к°Җ мӨ‘лӢЁлҗҳлҠ” л¬ём ңлҘј мһ¬нҳ„ н…ҢмҠӨнҠёлЎң кі м •н–ҲлӢӨ.
- gateway mail fetch л¬ём„ңмҷҖ env example м—җ мҡҙмҳҒ node лҠ” м ҲлҢҖ кІҪлЎңлҘј к¶ҢмһҘн•ҳлҗҳ, мғҒлҢҖ кІҪлЎңлҠ” env нҢҢмқј кё°мӨҖмқҙлқјлҠ” к·ңм№ҷмқ„ лӘ…мӢңн–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - always-on next action prompt м¶”к°Җ

- `ALWAYS_ON_NEXT_ACTION_PROMPT_V0.md` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ ліөмӮ¬/л¶ҷм—¬л„Јкё°к°Җ м–ҙл Өмҡҙ 24мӢңк°„ PC м—җм„ң м§§мқҖ нҢҢмқјлӘ… м§ҖмӢңл§ҢмңјлЎң post-review gateway м җкІҖкіј activity mirror лҘј мҲҳн–үн•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- bootstrap README м—җ prompt source лҘј мғүмқён•ҙ н•ӯмғҒ мјң л‘җлҠ” PC к°Җ pull нӣ„ лӢӨмқҢ мҡҙмҳҒ мһ‘м—…мқ„ нҢҢмқј кё°л°ҳмңјлЎң м°ҫкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - gateway healthcheck/healer нҢҗм • ліҙк°•

- `guild-hall:healer:run` мқҙ gateway fetch healthcheck JSON мқҳ `WARN`/`CRITICAL` мғҒнғңлҘј мӢӨнҢЁ м җкІҖмңјлЎң кё°лЎқн•ҙ activity carry-forward м—җ лӮЁкё°лҸ„лЎқ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- `gateway:fetch:healthcheck` к°Җ `EMAIL_FETCH_ALERT_TELEGRAM_ENABLED` мҷҖ `EMAIL_FETCH_ALERT_TELEGRAM_*` env м„Өм •мқ„ мӢӨм ң alert decision м—җ л°ҳмҳҒн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- Hiworks POP3 fetch к°Җ `last_uidl` мқҙнӣ„ л©”мӢңм§Җл¶Җн„° м§„н–үн•ҳкі , мӨ‘ліө мқҙлІӨнҠёмқҳ raw row лҘј л°ҳліө append н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ ліҙк°•н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - activity logger мҷҖ healer run кө¬нҳ„

- `guild-hall:activity:log` / `guild-hall:activity:refresh` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ лӘЁл“  PC к°Җ public-safe summary event лҘј кіөмҡ© activity surface м—җ лӮЁкёё мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- `guild-hall:healer:run` мқ„ м¶”к°Җн•ҙ 24мӢңк°„ PC к°Җ repo мғҒнғң, root validation, gateway fetch healthcheck кІ°кіјлҘј report/event/latest_context лЎң кё°лЎқн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- activity/healer лӢЁмң„ н…ҢмҠӨнҠёлҘј root validation harness м—җ м—°кІ°н•ҳкі , кҙҖл Ё README мҷҖ activity/multi-PC л¬ём„ңм—җ мӢӨн–ү кІҪкі„лҘј л°ҳмҳҒн–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - multi-PC node employee model м¶”к°Җ

- `MULTI_PC_DEVELOPMENT_V0.md` м—җ к°Ғ PC к°Җ bounded hotfix лҘј л§Ўмқ„ мҲҳ мһҲлҠ” node employee model мқ„ м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- 24мӢңк°„ мҡҙмҳҒмҡ© clone мқҖ clean `main` мңјлЎң мң м§Җн•ҳкі , к°„лӢЁ мҲҳм •мқҖ к°ҷмқҖ PC мқҳ лі„лҸ„ worktree/branch м—җм„ң мІҳлҰ¬н•ң л’Ө мҡҙмҳҒмҡ© clone мқҙ pull л°ӣлҠ” кө¬мЎ°лЎң м •лҰ¬н–ҲлӢӨ.

## 2026-05-07

### Revision `working` - play loop лі‘лӘ© мӣҗмқё кё°лЎқ м¶”к°Җ

- `PLAY_LOOP_V0` м—җ agent к°Җ stop condition к№Ңм§Җ м§„н–үн•  мҲҳ мһҲлҠ” мөңмҶҢ packet кё°мӨҖмқ„ м¶”к°Җн•ҙ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗк°Җ лӢӨмқҢ prompt лі‘лӘ©мқҙ лҗҳлҠ” м§Җм җмқ„ кё°лЎқн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- battle event м—җ `bottleneck_reason` мқ„ м¶”к°Җн•ҙ `intervention_count` к°Җ мҷң л°ңмғқн–ҲлҠ”м§Җ м§‘кі„н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- runner execution packet кіј snapshot next action м—җ anti-bottleneck loop лҘј м—°кІ°н•ҙ л°ҳліө лі‘лӘ©мқ„ workflow/mission handoff к°ңм„  нӣ„ліҙлЎң мҳ¬лҰ¬кІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - Hiworks POP3 long line мҲҳмӢ  ліҙк°•

- Hiworks POP3 `RETR` мҲҳмӢ м—җм„ң Python `poplib` кё°ліё 2048 byte line limit м—җ кұёлҰ¬м§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ connector-local long-line reader лҘј м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- `HIWORKS_POP3_MAX_LINE_BYTES` env м„Өм •кіј synthetic long-line н…ҢмҠӨнҠёлҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ raw mail body м—Ҷмқҙ кёҙ лқјмқё мҲҳмӢ  кІҪлЎңлҘј кІҖмҰқн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - gateway mail fetch operator м¶ңл Ҙ redaction

- `gateway:fetch` run summary/debug/CLI error output м—җ raw mail body, HTML, URL, token-like cursor к°Җ м„һм—¬лҸ„ operator terminal м—җ к·ёлҢҖлЎң л…ём¶ңлҗҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ sanitize кІҪлЎңлҘј м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- 24мӢңк°„ PC `email -> monster` smoke prompt лҠ” live fetch м—җм„ң `--json` мқ„ мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  count/status мӨ‘мӢ¬мңјлЎң нҷ•мқён•ҳлҸ„лЎқ мЎ°м •н–ҲлӢӨ.

- к°ҷмқҖ repo лҘј м—¬лҹ¬ PC к°Җ clone н•ҙлҸ„ `guild_hall/state/**`, `_workspaces/**`, `_workmeta/**`, `private-state/**`, public `Soulforge` мқҳ primary writer к°Җ кІ№м№ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ н‘ңмҷҖ мӨ‘ліө л°©м§Җ к·ңм№ҷмқ„ ліҙк°•н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - doctor local node identity м җкІҖ м¶”к°Җ

- `operator`, `owner-with-state` н”„лЎңн•„м—җм„ңлҠ” local node identity лҘј н•„мҲҳлЎң ліҙкі , `public-only` м—җм„ңлҠ” missing мқ„ н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳлҗҳ кІ°кіјм—җ н‘ңмӢңн•ңлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - work PC bootstrap prompt м¶”к°Җ

- `docs/architecture/bootstrap/WORK_PC_BOOTSTRAP_PROMPT_V0.md` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ м—…л¬ҙ PC к°Җ Git pull нӣ„ Codex м—җкІҢ нҢҢмқј кё°л°ҳ `work_pc` bootstrap м§ҖмӢңлҘј л°ӣмқ„ мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- prompt лҠ” мӢӨм ң н”„лЎңм қнҠё нҢҢмқјкіј `_workmeta` кё°лЎқмқ„ лӢӨлЈЁлҠ” м—…л¬ҙ PC м—ӯн• мқ„ м„Өм •н•ҳлҗҳ, always-on scheduler мҷҖ кі м„ұлҠҘ tool мһ‘м—…мқҖ кё°ліё м°ЁлӢЁн•ҳлҸ„лЎқ м •лҰ¬н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - always-on node bootstrap prompt м¶”к°Җ

- `docs/architecture/bootstrap/ALWAYS_ON_NODE_BOOTSTRAP_PROMPT_V0.md` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ 24мӢңк°„ мҡҙмҳҒ PC к°Җ Git pull нӣ„ Codex м—җкІҢ нҢҢмқј кё°л°ҳ bootstrap м§ҖмӢңлҘј л°ӣмқ„ мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- bootstrap README м—җ prompt source лҘј мғүмқён•ҙ кёҙ нҷ”л©ҙкіөмң  л¶ҷм—¬л„Јкё° м—Ҷмқҙ `always_on_node` local identity, doctor, snapshot, night_watch preflight м Ҳм°ЁлҘј м°ҫкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

- `AUTOHUNT_MODEL.md`, `NIGHT_WATCH_AUTOMATION_V0.md`, `PROJECT_MAP_V0.md` лҘј кё°мЎҙ owner мІҙкі„ м•Ҳм—җм„ң м—°кІ°н•ҙ мғҲ мөңмғҒмң„ лҚӨн”„ л¬ём„ң м—Ҷмқҙ node capability / 24мӢңк°„ мҡҙмҳҒ / мһҗлҸҷмӮ¬лғҘ нҷ•мһҘм„ мқ„ м°ҫкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

- `soulforge_snapshot.json` м—җ `source_observations` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ UI к°Җ ліҙлҠ” snapshot мқҙ м–ҙл–Ө мӣҗліё metadata кё°мӨҖмқём§Җ нҢҗм •н•  мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- `npm run guild-hall:snapshot:check-fresh` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ м ҖмһҘлҗң local snapshot кіј нҳ„мһ¬ мӣҗліё surface мқҳ fingerprint mismatch лҘј к°җм§Җн•ҳкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- freshness кҙҖмёЎ лІ”мң„лҠ” repo metadata, roadmap, mission index, `_workspaces`, `_workmeta`, gateway state, private-state surface лЎң м ңн•ңн•ҳкі  мӣҗліё м—…л¬ҙ лӮҙмҡ©мқҖ мқҪм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - read-only Soulforge snapshot producer м¶”к°Җ

- кё°ліё м¶ңл ҘмқҖ local-only `guild_hall/state/snapshot/soulforge_snapshot.json` мңјлЎң л‘җкі , raw mailbox, attachment, token, `_workspaces` нҢҢмқј лӮҙмҡ©мқҖ snapshot м—җ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ кІҪкі„лҘј кі м •н–ҲлӢӨ.
- `validate:snapshot` мқ„ root acceptance м—җ м—°кІ°н•ҙ snapshot shape мҷҖ private content л№„л…ём¶ң мөңмҶҢ test лҘј н•Ёк»ҳ лҸҢлҰ¬кІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

## 2026-03-27

- мғҲ `operator` н”„лЎңн•„мқ„ м¶”к°Җн•ҙ private repo м—ҶмқҙлҸ„ gateway/town_crier local env мҷҖ smoke/live лҘј лӢӨлЈ° мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- `owner-with-state` лҠ” кі„мҶҚ `_workmeta/`, `private-state/` мҷҖ continuity restore лҘј мҡ”кө¬н•ҳлҠ” owner м „мҡ© н”„лЎңн•„лЎң мң м§Җн–ҲлӢӨ.

- canonical entrypoint лҠ” `npm run guild-hall:validate:canon` мңјлЎң л‘җкі , convenience alias лЎң `npm run canon:validate` лҘј н•Ёк»ҳ м ңкіөн•ңлӢӨ.
- mission мқҳ `workflow_id: null` мҳҲмҷёк°Җ readiness blocked к·ңм№ҷкіј л§һлҠ”м§ҖлҸ„ мІ« validator лІ”мң„м—җ нҸ¬н•Ён–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - class title мқ„ м„ёкі„кҙҖ нҶӨмңјлЎң ліҙм •

- `archivist` мқҳ мӮ¬лһҢмҡ© title мқ„ `кё°лЎқкҙҖ` мңјлЎң, `administrator` мқҳ мӮ¬лһҢмҡ© title мқ„ `мҙқкҙҖ` мңјлЎң мЎ°м •н–ҲлӢӨ.
- лӮҙл¶Җ `class_id` лҠ” к·ёлҢҖлЎң мң м§Җн•ҳкі , world-facing м„ӨлӘ…л§Ң мЎ°м •н•ҙ кё°мЎҙ unit/workflow binding кіј кІҪлЎңлҘј к№Ём§Җ м•ҠкІҢ мң м§Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- `human` species hero мҷҖ guild master кҙҖл Ё м„ӨлӘ…лҸ„ governance / archive нҶӨмңјлЎң к°ҷмқҙ л§һм·„лӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - ontology review мғҒкё° manual кіј guild_master carry-forward к·ңм№ҷ м¶”к°Җ

- `docs/architecture/foundation/ONTOLOGY_REVIEW_MANUAL_V0.md` лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҙ ontology review trigger, м ҖмһҘ мң„м№ҳ, carry-forward owner лҘј кі м •н–ҲлӢӨ.
- root `AGENTS.md` мҷҖ `night_watch` л¬ём„ң/prompt м—җ ontology candidate мғҒкё° к·ңм№ҷмқ„ л„Јм–ҙ, нҳ„мһ¬ н”„лЎңм қнҠёк°Җ м•„лӢҲм–ҙлҸ„ `guild_master` / `night_watch` lane мқҙ cross-project нӣ„ліҙлҘј лӢӨмӢң л– мҳ¬лҰ¬кІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.
- activity surface м—җлҠ” ontology review candidate лҘј `carry_forward: true` лЎң лӮЁкёё мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨлҠ” к·ңм№ҷмқ„ м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - ontology-style м ҖмһҘ к·ңм№ҷ кё°мӨҖм„  м¶”к°Җ

- Soulforge н•өмӢ¬ к°ңл…җмқ„ `к°ңмІҙ + кҙҖкі„` кё°мӨҖмңјлЎң мқҪлҠ” `Ontology Model v0` foundation л¬ём„ңлҘј м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- ontology м •мқҳмҷҖ кҙҖкі„ к·ңм№ҷмқҖ public foundation л¬ём„ңк°Җ л“Өкі , project-specific instance лҠ” `_workmeta/<project_code>/ontology/` м—җ л‘җл©°, runtime event лҠ” кі„мҶҚ `guild_hall/state/**` мҷҖ `private-state/**` к°Җ мҶҢмң н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ м ҖмһҘ мң„м№ҳлҘј кі м •н–ҲлӢӨ.
- мғҲ top-level `ontology/` root лҠ” л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•Ҡкі , кё°мЎҙ owner root м•Ҳм—җм„ң м •мқҳ/canon instance/runtime event лҘј л¶„лҰ¬н•ҳлҠ” л°©н–ҘмңјлЎң м •лҰ¬н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - starter class lineup мқ„ 6мў…мңјлЎң нҷ•мһҘ

- кё°мЎҙ `knight`, `archivist`, `administrator` м—җ лҚ”н•ҙ `pathfinder`, `marshal`, `auditor` canonical class sample 3мў…мқ„ м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- мғҲ class л“ӨмқҖ species мҷҖ лҸ…лҰҪлҗң м¶•мқ„ мң м§Җн•ҳкі , мӢӨм ң мЎ°н•©мқҖ кі„мҶҚ unit/party/workflow/mission м—җм„ң кІ°м •н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ мң м§Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- ref лҠ” кё°мЎҙ `.registry/skills`, `.registry/tools`, `.registry/knowledge` canon м•Ҳм—җм„ңл§Ң мЎ°н•©н•ҙ `м •м°°`, `м§‘н–ү`, `кІҖмҰқ` lane мқ„ л“ңлҹ¬лӮҙлҸ„лЎқ л§һм·„лӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - night_watch preflight м—җ transient retry м¶”к°Җ

- `night_watch` current-default pipeline мқҳ preflight лҠ” кі„мҶҚ `fail-closed` лЎң мң м§Җн•ҳлҗҳ, dirty repo, detached HEAD, missing origin, non-main branch лҠ” мҰүмӢң hard fail н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ лӘ…мӢңн–ҲлӢӨ.
- л°ҳлҢҖлЎң DNS н•ҙм„қ мӢӨнҢЁ, temporary name resolution failure, timeout, connection reset, TLS handshake timeout, network unreachable, transient 5xx gateway мҳӨлҘҳ к°ҷмқҖ мқјмӢңм Ғ network-class мӢӨнҢЁлҠ” bounded retry л’Ө мөңмў… нҢҗм •н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ к·ңм№ҷмқ„ м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- repo sync лҠ” мөңлҢҖ 3нҡҢ мӢңлҸ„, doctor remote кІҖмӮ¬лҠ” repo sync м„ұкіө нӣ„ 1нҡҢ мһ¬мӢңлҸ„л§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳкі , к·ёлһҳлҸ„ мӢӨнҢЁн•ҳл©ҙ blocked preflight лЎң мӨ‘лӢЁн•ҳкІҢ prompt/source мҷҖ мҡҙмҳҒ л¬ём„ңлҘј л§һм·„лӢӨ.

## 2026-03-26

### Revision `working` - мў…мЎұ м§Ғм—… лӘ¬мҠӨн„°мқҳ мӮ¬лһҢмҡ© н•ңкёҖ н‘ңмӢң к·ңм№ҷ м¶”к°Җ

- canonical id лҠ” кі„мҶҚ stable ASCII лҘј мң м§Җн•ҳкі , мӮ¬лһҢм—җкІҢ ліҙм—¬мЈјлҠ” мқҙлҰ„мқҖ `title`, `display_name`, `monster_label` к°ҷмқҖ human-facing н•„л“ңм—җ н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң л‘ҳ мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨлҠ” к·ңм№ҷмқ„ public canon л¬ём„ңм—җ м¶”к°Җн–ҲлӢӨ.
- current sample species/class title кіј human hero title мқ„ н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң л°”кҝЁлӢӨ.
- `monster` кі„м—ҙмқҖ `monster_family` / `monster_name` / `monster_type` id лҘј мң м§Җн•ҳлҗҳ, candidate note мҷҖ lineup л¬ём„ңм—җм„ң optional `monster_label` лЎң н•ңкөӯм–ҙ н‘ңмӢңлҘј л‘ҳ мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ н–ҲлӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - species мҷҖ class лҸ…лҰҪ мЎ°н•© к·ңм№ҷ м¶”к°Җ

- `.registry` canon м—җм„ң species мҷҖ class лҠ” м„ңлЎң мў…мҶҚлҗҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” лҸ…лҰҪ catalog м¶•мқҙлқјкі  лӘ…мӢңн–ҲлӢӨ.
- мӢӨм ң мЎ°н•©мқҖ `.unit/<unit_id>/unit.yaml` мқҳ `identity.species_id + class_ids` к°Җ кІ°м •н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ л¬ём„ңмҷҖ schema лҘј м •лҰ¬н–ҲлӢӨ.
- к·ёлһҳм„ң `orc + knight` к°ҷмқҖ мЎ°н•©лҸ„ canon мғҒ н—Ҳмҡ©лҗҳл©°, м ңн•ңмқҙ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©ҙ unit/party/workflow/mission м—җм„ңл§Ң н‘ңнҳ„н•ҳлҸ„лЎқ к·ңм№ҷмқ„ кі м •н–ҲлӢӨ.
- starter species lineup мқҖ `human`, `orc`, `elf`, `dwarf`, `darkelf` 5мў…мңјлЎң л§һм·„лӢӨ.

### Revision `working` - agent procedure capture entrypoint rule

- Added a root `AGENTS.md` rule so every bounded business task leaves tracked promotion-ready evidence in `_workmeta/<project_code>/reports/**` instead of relying on chat memory or ignored runtime logs.
- Kept `AGENTS.md` as the short routing surface and pointed detailed capture fields to `_workmeta/PROCEDURE_CAPTURE_RULE.md`, including repeatable steps, decision criteria, folder or packet shape, and completion criteria for later promotion into `skill`, `workflow`, `mission`, `role_or_class`, or `data_contract`.

- мқҙ ліҖкІҪмңјлЎң automation prompt м—…лҚ°мқҙнҠё мһҗмІҙлҠ” Git нҳ•мғҒкҙҖлҰ¬лҗҳкі , лӢӨлҘё PC лҠ” repo pull нӣ„ к°ҷмқҖ source лҘј ліҙкі  local automation мқ„ лӢӨмӢң install н•  мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ.
